***mobiel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mobiel.html>mobiel</a> (5076)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">mobile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mōbilis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">easy to be moved, moveable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">moveō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">move</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mobiel.html>mobiel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mobiel.html>mobieler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">mobielst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mobile</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mobiel.html>mobiel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mobiel.html>mobielen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mobieltje.html>mobieltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mobile phone, cellphone, mobile.</li>
<li>A mobile <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">kinetic arrangement</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>

***mocha.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>mocha</a> (63960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mocha,_Yemen" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mocha, Yemen"><a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>Mocha</a>, Yemen</a>, a port on the Red Sea, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">اَلْمُخَا</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">al-muḵā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, due to its being a major marketplace for coffee during Ottoman rule.
</p><p>The <a href = vnd.unilang:beans.html>beans</a> often <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a chocolaty flavor, hence by extension <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to refer to any coffee with a chocolate flavor, or any mixture of coffee and chocolate flavors, notably coffee with chocolate syrup added.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>mocha</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mochas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A coffee <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> with chocolate syrup added, or a serving thereof; a caffè <a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>mocha</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">caffè <a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>mocha</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">mochaccino</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A coffee and chocolate mixed flavour.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>mocha</a></b> fudge</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A dark brown colour, like that of <a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>mocha</a> coffee.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>mocha</a> colour: <span style="background-color:50473F; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A strong Arabian coffee.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An Abyssinian weight, equivalent to a <a href = vnd.unilang:troy.html>Troy</a> grain.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mochaccino</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>mocha</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of a dark brown colour, like that of <a href = vnd.unilang:mocha.html>mocha</a> coffee.</li></ol>
</body>

***mockingbird.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mockingbird.html>mockingbird</a> (60032)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mocking</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bird</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mockingbird.html>mockingbird</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mockingbirds</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A long-tailed American songbird of the Mimidae family, noted for its ability to mimic calls of other <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">mocker</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>the family Mimidae (mimids) also includes thrashers, tremblers and the New World catbirds.</li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:modderfiguur.html>modderfiguur</a> (74300)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:modder.html>modder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:figuur.html>figuur</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:modderfiguur.html>modderfiguur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:modderfiguur.html>modderfiguren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:modderfiguur.html>modderfiguurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A silly, ridiculous character, <span class="use-with-mention">mainly used in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:modderfiguur.html>modderfiguur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>.</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A shape or symbol made in mud.</li>

***moddergevecht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moddergevecht.html>moddergevecht</a> (102884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:modder.html>modder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gevecht.html>gevecht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a fight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <a href = vnd.unilang:vechten.html>vechten</a> 'to fight')
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moddergevecht.html>moddergevecht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moddergevecht.html>moddergevechten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moddergevecht.html>moddergevechttje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mud fight, where opponents wrestle in mud or other dirt</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A dirty <a href = vnd.unilang:duel.html>duel</a>, involving verbal mudslinging</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:moddergevecht.html>moddergevecht</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moe.html>moe</a> (870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moede.html>moede</a></i> with loss of <i>-d-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:moede.html>moede</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tired, loath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">muothi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tired</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mōþaz</i>.
Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">müde</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mēþe</i>.
</p>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>This word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually used predicatively rather than attributively. If an attributive sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> needed, most people use <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermoeid.html>vermoeid</a></i>. The forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeien.html>moeie</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">moeier</i> are often proscribed. The form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moede.html>moede</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mostly formal.
</p>

***moed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moed.html>moed</a> (1601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*muot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mōdaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moed.html>moed</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">courage</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">bravery</span>, daring</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">mood</span>; internal nature, mental disposition
<ul><li><b>1628</b>, Philips Marnix <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sint.html>Sint</a> Aldegonde, "Wilhelmus <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Nassouwe", (modern, redacted version), <a href = vnd.unilang:couplet.html>couplet</a> 7.

***moedertaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moedertaal.html>moedertaal</a> (30372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">language</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense “mother tongue” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> initially only used as a genitival noun phrase <i><a href = vnd.unilang:moeders.html>moeders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">moederstaal</i>, whence <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">moerstaal</i>; spellings without interfix <i>-s-</i> become normal for this sense in the 18th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***moer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a> (5043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> by syncope of medial <span class="IPA">/d/</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeren.html>moeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moertje.html>moertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mother</li>
<li>a queen bee</li>
<li>a female <a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a></li>
<li>a female rabbit</li>
<li>a female ferret</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">mother</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ma.html>ma</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mama.html>mama</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">queen bee</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijenkoningin.html>bijenkoningin</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">female <a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">moershaas</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">female rabbit</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">moerkonijn</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hellemoer</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">moershaas</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">moerkonijn</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">moerschroef</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schroef.html>schroef</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bolt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeren.html>moeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moertje.html>moertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a type of fastener with a threaded hole; a <a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something small and insignificant (in the phrase <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a></i>)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schelen.html>schelen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I do not care at all.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a></i>, a dialectal variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:modder.html>modder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeren.html>moeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moertje.html>moertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sediment formed in various alcoholic drinks and vinegar; compare French: mère <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vinaigre</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">morass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mōraz</i>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">moor</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mōr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">moor, marsh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moer.html>moer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeren.html>moeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moertje.html>moertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>morass, marsh, peat</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moerassen.html>moerassen</a> (21282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***moeten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> (86)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">muotan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mōtaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mote</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">may, might</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be necessary, to be required</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have to, must
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> to</b> / He <b>must</b> go.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>Moest</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a> you <b>have to</b> work tonight?</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verplicht.html>verplicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> should, be meant to, be supposed to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gestolen.html>gestolen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> meant to</b> be here, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a>. / It <b>should</b> be here, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You really <b>should</b> not do that.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> 1 <a href = vnd.unilang:januari.html>januari</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:werking.html>werking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:treden.html>treden</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The new law <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> supposed to</b> come into force on 1 January.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have to go, to need to go, must go
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:supermarkt.html>supermarkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I still <b>need to go</b> to the supermarket today.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need to go to the <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nodig.html>nodig</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I really <b>need to go</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The past tense <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a></i> can be used in the present. In Dutch, one can ask "<span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>Moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a>?</span>" which can mean both "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a></b> you have to work tonight?" and "<b>do</b> you have to work tonight?". This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> similar to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:modaal.html>modaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>werkwoord</a></span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:gedwongen.html>gedwongen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wc.html>wc</a>.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brommen.html>brommen</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***mof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mof.html>mof</a> (14530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">moffel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">moufle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">muffula</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mof.html>mof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moffen.html>moffen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mof.html>mofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:muff.html>muff</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plumbing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Piece to protect pipes where they are poorly connected.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:muff.html>Muff</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a> (472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mugan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maganą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*magʰ-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*megʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toegestaan.html>toegestaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may, can, be allowed to

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> may go, can go, to be allowed to go

***mogendheid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mogendheid.html>mogendheid</a> (74286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mogentheit</i>. Equivalent to the present participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogendheid.html>mogendheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogendheden.html>mogendheden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogendheid.html>mogendheidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> power, powerhouse <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">polity that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> regionally or internationally powerful in a given field</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grootmacht.html>grootmacht</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:macht.html>macht</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> power, might

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moker.html>moker</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>a blow from a sledgehammer
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leek.html>leek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alsof.html>alsof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mokerslag.html>mokerslag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:getroffen.html>getroffen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>It felt like I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> struck by a sledgehammer.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crushing blow, winning hit</li></ol>

***mokken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mokken.html>mokken</a> (13556)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">muckezzen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pout</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">mucken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grouse, to grumble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:West Germanic languages">West Germanic</a></span> onomatopoeic origin.  Probably not related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mugio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I bellow, <a href = vnd.unilang:moo.html>moo</a>, bray</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>mol</a> (5820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>mol</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>mol</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>mol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mollen.html>mollen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mol.html>molletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">mole</span>, any insectivore of the family Talpidae.</li>
<li>A <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_mole" class="extiw" title="w:European mole">European mole</a>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Talpa_europaea" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Talpa europaea"><i>Talpa europaea</i></a></span>.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">mole</span>, an <span class="Latn" lang="en">infiltrator</span>, an <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:infiltrant.html>infiltrant</a></span>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">molécule</i>, a modern diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">moles</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
